WHEN NOT MATCHED THEN
INSERT ([CategoryId], [Code], [CreatedAt], [Description], [Discount], [Image], [Latest], [Name], [Price], [ProductDate], [Quantity], [Special], [Unit], [UpdatedAt], [Views])
VALUES (i.[CategoryId], i.[Code], i.[CreatedAt], i.[Description], i.[Discount], i.[Image], i.[Latest], i.[Name], i.[Price], i.[ProductDate], i.[Quantity], i.[Special], i.[Unit], i.[UpdatedAt], i.[Views])
OUTPUT INSERTED.[Id], i._Position
INTO @inserted0;

SELECT [t].[Id] FROM [Products] t
INNER JOIN @inserted0 i ON ([t].[Id] = [i].[Id])
ORDER BY [i].[_Position];
